\DoxyCodeLine{02533\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ A\ descriptor\ that\ contains\ information\ about\ formatting\ arguments.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02534\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ the\ number\ of\ arguments\ is\ less\ or\ equal\ to\ max\_packed\_args\ then}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02535\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ argument\ types\ are\ passed\ in\ the\ descriptor.\ This\ reduces\ binary\ code\ size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02536\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ per\ formatting\ function\ call.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02537\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{long}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{long}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__format__args_adec0b23c6fe57883ccb17d99b1498753}{desc\_}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{02538\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{union\ }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02539\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ If\ is\_packed()\ returns\ true\ then\ argument\ values\ are\ stored\ in\ values\_;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02540\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ otherwise\ they\ are\ stored\ in\ args\_.\ This\ is\ done\ to\ improve\ cache}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02541\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ locality\ and\ reduce\ compiled\ code\ size\ since\ storing\ larger\ objects}}
